  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0ef47f39-b1d0-492f-b743-08e4d037ddcd'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I just saw this on Rick`s webpage.<br/>A. Because of your interest, I decided to write a series of short stories in which the Kane children meet the demigo<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I just saw this on Rick`s webpage.<br />A. Because of your interest, I decided to write a series of short stories in which the Kane children meet the demigods. In the first, "The Son of Sobek," Carter Kane meets Percy Jackson.In the second, "The Staff of Serapis," Sadie Kane meets Annabeth Chase. The third crossover story will be out in 2015, and will bring all four characters together. The first two stories are available as e-singles, and also appear in the paperback versions of Mark of Athena (for Sobek) and House of Hades (for Serapis.) <br /><br /><br />hope that helps.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2852216849072473001"><br/>I enjoyed this even much more than I did the first book. I love that it’s about Sadie and Annabeth, two of my favorite heroines in Uncle Ricky’s epic adventure stories. I love how the story opened up with a bang and ended up with the same and as usual, Uncle Ricky’s imaginative and hilarious descriptions kept me entertained the entire reading time. I was almost clapping when my most awaited moment arrived- when the villainous god finally said “GAH!” and “RAR!” <br/><br/>P.S. Happy early birthday, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1099868891?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra!</a>.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16226373726482354972"><b> <u>After Reading</u> </b><br/><br/>First of all. VERY FIRST OF ALL. I wanna just shout out to the world that MY ONLY TWO PREDICTIONS about this two short stories HAVE COME TRUE!! These two are-<br/><br/>1. I knew, I FREAKING KNEW that <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ these two short stories were AFTER the Heroes of Olympus series. Psshh, fans making weird assumptions that magicians will pop out in HoO series- no offense but Are you nuts?  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/>2. My assumption was that <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Setne could be behind the Son of Sobek story, a</span></span>
  <span id="freeText16226373726482354972" style="display:none"><b> <u>After Reading</u> </b><br><br>First of all. VERY FIRST OF ALL. I wanna just shout out to the world that MY ONLY TWO PREDICTIONS about this two short stories HAVE COME TRUE!! These two are-<br><br>1. I knew, I FREAKING KNEW that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ these two short stories were AFTER the Heroes of Olympus series. Psshh, fans making weird assumptions that magicians will pop out in HoO series- no offense but Are you nuts?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>2. My assumption was that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Setne could be behind the Son of Sobek story, and Voila, it all came out true in this story!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>*sniffle* I feel so Proud to know Uncle Rick That well!<br><br>Also, please don't kill me when I say that the story wasn't intriguing to me at first. Like we're all pretty used to weird monsters right? But after meeting Sadie Kane, and ALL that funny-horrendous-awesome-terrifying Adventure, it deserves SO much more than mere 5 stars!! So just like all Uncle Rick fans, I wanna thank him SO SO much for this AMAZING story!<br><br>Oh what else? I also wanna smack him upside the head for <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ not letting Sadie know about Carter's adventure. Do you want my favorite character to burn to death from Sadie's stare??  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>But apart from ALL that, I'm pretty sure Rick would be sitting there proudly ALL like<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400588258ra/9692512.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I applause you dude! Especially for his <u>Brilliant Knowledge</u> he has stored in some secret part of his brain. For example- Serapis. From which part of this entire cosmos did Rick plucked him out and pasted in his story? Gosh, seriously, where does Rick makes such a detailed research?? I SO wanna know!<br><br>All right, fangirl mode off. To the readers of both the PJO, HoO and Kane Chronicles series, it might be a Deja Vu a little to get reminded of ALL those adventures the demigods and magicians did back in their own series. It was definitely a plus point of this book. And of course Rick's way of describing things is flawless! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I mean the God wearing a swimming trunk and a flower pot hat? Awesome description! (no sarcasm dude)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I could actually go on praising my favorite writer in the world again and again, but let's come back to the story :P. <br>Annabeth Chase and Sadie Kane, both blonde, both with certain attitudes (in a good way), and confident. What a great pair! Certainly better than Carter-Percy pair, when the boys just decided to throw rage over each other for no apparent reason (psshh...typical boys). <br>The best part of the story was that it was so <i>Awe-inspiring</i>.<br><br>So Excited to know more! A few more crossovers would certainly do, like-<br>Nico and Anubis/Walt<br>Khufu and Grover<br>Coach Hedge and Bes (DIIIEEE!!!)<br>Bast and...Frank?<br>Felix and Leo!<br>Leo and ZIA!<br>Jason and..Shu..i guess. Or that Russian dude..Leonid!<br><br>Okay I shouldn't try more, but these would be great. Or even greater- <u>A whole new series!</u>. I'm really Excited for a series of books that unfolds ALL the Greco-Egyptian period and its impact on the heroes of the generation.<br><br>Aaaannnd AT LAST, a few <u> OMG moments </u> for me to freak out with the fangirls out there. I hope they sympathize well enough with me to read my further freak-out rantings :). These were my very first reactions, and they may be a bit too much, but if you've read both the series, you'll understand it well, because it was THE Annabeth Chase on one side and THE Sadie Kane on another!! :D<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>OMG- Sadie's British style Entry!!<br>OMG- Annabeth thinks she's like her?? GET A PURPLE HIGHLIGHT LADY! You don't know her!!<br>OMG- They didn't fight! *Phew*<br>OMG- WoW, they just got over this new world they found, it's really good for them...THANK FATES no sobbing or crying.<br>OMG- Annabeth thinks Sadie would go along her 'friends'. Are these the Seven of the Prophecy dudes????? And girls???? Is she mentioning Leo Valdez here???<br>OMG- ANNABETH MENTIONED FRANK AAAAAAAAHHHHHHHH I LOVE YOU FRANK ZHANG!!! I LOVE HIM FOR REVEALING THE CROSSOVER'S TIMELINE!!!!<br>OMG- Annabeth drank healing potion and Sadie had ambrosia. Aww Sadie we KNOW how much you LOVE your Grandma's scones :D<br>OMG- Annabeth sarcastically thinking of Sadie making chalk drawings- those were my exact thinking right then, even though I knew what she was up to :P<br>OMG- 'In the sea, suffer misery' to 'In the sea, suffer moss!' gave me ten minute hysterical laughing and seven minutes concerned glare of family members.<br>OMG- ANNABETH DRANK RIBENA!!! *hugs*<br>OMG- :O. Annabeth thought the ship was ARGO 2?!?!?!?!?!<br>OMG- OMG OMG THEY HUGGED!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! &lt;3 &lt;3<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><u> After Cover release </u><br><br>o.O Is that what I think it is?? IS THIS ANNABETH?!?! Wow, we've Never seen Annabeth in a book cover before!!! OH MY GOSH these Two girls look more like Long-lost-sisters here :DDD.<br><br>Wait, why is there hieroglyphs 'around' Annabeth?? Or is it aimed on the two-face-one-butt monster? And what is that animal Behind Sadie?? A dog with snake tail? And OMG is the Fight gonna happen IN the METRO?!?! Or would they just MEET and Greet in there?? Gosh, SO MUCH TO KNOW!!!!!!<br><br><u> When the announcement just came up </u><br><br>When i heard about it, i first screamed for like 5 minutes (a fangirl has her own ways to satisfy herself :D) !! I mean come on guys the meeting of Annabeth Chase and Sadie Kane would be 10 times as dangerous as Percy and Carter Meeting right? <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14372710221263759726"><strong>“That’s okay,” Annabeth said. “How are you at bluffing, lying, and trash-talking?”<br/>Sadie raised an eyebrow. “I’ve been told those are my most attractive qualities.”<br/>“Excellent,” Annabeth said. “Then it’s time I taught you some Greek.”</strong><br/><br/>Ok so two strong, god-spitting badass blonde women fighting side to side... what a wonderful world we are living in.<br/><br/>5/5⭐️</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText1587654608307666486" style="display:none">It's Annabeth's POV. I could almost stop right there, because Annabeth. But since I'm here, I'll add that Sadie seems to have matured an incredible amount since the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12893742.The_Serpent_s_Shadow__Kane_Chronicles___3_" title="The Serpent's Shadow (Kane Chronicles, #3) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Serpent's Shadow</a>. But she really kind of had to for this story to work. She would have looked even more vapid than she sometimes did in her own series. But this version of Sadie is actually a match for Annabeth. Which makes the realization that this is probably going to turn into a series of short stories with a connected storyline exciting. I look forward to seeing who will meet next.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer756854305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7655519747365784573">Rick Riordon HAS to write a series combining Greek and Egyptian mythology. Seriously, he already started a whole new era with this "Crown of Ptolemy" thing. I gotta have more. This is epic, okay. How old is Sadie again? I thought she was at least 14 or something...but it mentioned in here "no older than 13" what? my memory sucks. <br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote> “Oh, I believe you. It’s too ridiculous not to be true. It’s just that each time my world gets stranger, I think: Right. We’re at maximum oddness now. At least I kn</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText7655519747365784573" style="display:none">Rick Riordon HAS to write a series combining Greek and Egyptian mythology. Seriously, he already started a whole new era with this "Crown of Ptolemy" thing. I gotta have more. This is epic, okay. How old is Sadie again? I thought she was at least 14 or something...but it mentioned in here "no older than 13" what? my memory sucks. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote> “Oh, I believe you. It’s too ridiculous not to be true. It’s just that each time my world gets stranger, I think: Right. We’re at maximum oddness now. At least I know the full extent of it. First, I find out my brother and I are descended from the pharaohs and have magic powers. All right. No problem. Then I find out my dead father has merged his soul with Osiris and become the lord of the dead. Brilliant! Why not? Then my uncle takes over the House of Life and oversees hundreds of magicians around the world. Then my boyfriend turns out to be a hybrid magician boy/immortal god of funerals. And all the while I’m thinking, Of course! Keep calm and carry on! I’ve adjusted! And then you come along on a random Thursday, la-di-da, and say, Oh, by the way, Egyptian gods are just one small part of the cosmic absurdity. We’ve also got the Greeks to worry about! Hooray!”<br /><br />“That’s okay,’ Annabeth said. ‘How are you at bluffing, lying and trash-talking?’<br />Sadie raised an eyebrow. ‘I’ve been told those are my most attractive qualities.”<br /><br />“Forge ahead,’ Sadie said. ‘Think on my feet. When necessary, blast enemies into teeny-tiny bits.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />--your lovely Sadie Kane at work</span>

<div id="review_1362573953" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1362573953" />
    <a title="Jesica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44637869-jesica"><img alt="Jesica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469336667p2/44637869.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1362573953?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jesica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jesica" href="/user/show/44637869-jesica">Jesica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1362573953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18378201538364204349">Another crossover between <i>The Heroes of Olympus</i> and <i>The Kane Chronicles</i> series. After Percy met Carter in <i>The Son of Sobek</i>, now it’s Annabeth and Sadie’s turn.<br/><br/>Annabeth was on her way home after an interview for internship at a local architecture firm when she saw a weird monster and decided to follow it and met Sadie Kane who was fighting a similar monster.<br/><br/>The story follows Annabeth. I love this girls team more than the boys one. Annabeth and Sadie proved a lot better pair than Percy and Carter.</span>
  <span id="freeText18378201538364204349" style="display:none">Another crossover between <i>The Heroes of Olympus</i> and <i>The Kane Chronicles</i> series. After Percy met Carter in <i>The Son of Sobek</i>, now it’s Annabeth and Sadie’s turn.<br /><br />Annabeth was on her way home after an interview for internship at a local architecture firm when she saw a weird monster and decided to follow it and met Sadie Kane who was fighting a similar monster.<br /><br />The story follows Annabeth. I love this girls team more than the boys one. Annabeth and Sadie proved a lot better pair than Percy and Carter. There’s no accidental stupid fight and they communicated better too. They became friends almost immediately. The enemy was interesting too. While the Son of Sobek was 100 percent Egyptian, Serapis was both Egyptian and Greek. I didn’t know such god exist. And while Percy and Carter’s meeting was set up by someone to see if they’d fight, Annabeth and Sadie’s meeting was pure coincident. This short story is very entertaining. The combination of Sadie’s magic and Annabeth’s wisdom was so wonderful (for the second time since the chinese handcuff, when fighting an impossible foe, Annabeth was inspired by Frank Zhang. I laughed when she suddenly remembered Frank’s quote :p). And also it’s fun to imagine what would happened to Carter when Sadie gets back to Brooklyn House.<br /><blockquote>‘Percy told me a crazy story about meeting a boy out near Moriches Bay. Apparently this kid used hieroglyphs to cast spells. He helped Percy battle a big crocodile monster.’<br />‘The Son of Sobek!’ Sadie blurted. ‘But my brother battled that monster. He didn’t say anything about –’<br />‘Is your brother’s name Carter?’ Annabeth asked.<br />An angry golden aura flickered around Sadie’s head – a halo of hieroglyphs that resembled frowns, fists and dead stick men.<br />‘As of this moment,’ Sadie growled, ‘my brother’s name is Punching Bag. Seems he hasn’t been telling me everything.’</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="18378201538364204349" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27353893-romane?shelf=crossover">crossover</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1007993383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7793835029700822524"><i>Sadie + Annabeth</i>, ultimate girl power!<br/><br/>Wow, I'm literally hyperventilating right now because of how really great this book is. I mean, Rick Riordan writes so well. Simply the best. <br/><br/>When I read the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17312201.The_Son_of_Sobek__Percy_Jackson___Kane_Chronicles_Crossover___1_' title='The Son of Sobek (Percy Jackson & Kane Chronicles Crossover, #1) by Rick Riordan' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Son of Sobek</a>, I was really amazed by the crossover. Two of my favorite fictional crushes combined? That is what you call fantastic.<br/><br/>And then I read this book. Oh gods, I couldn't ask for more. It was really a great read, two different worlds are combined into a single story. Perfect.<br/><br/>I really hope Ric</span>
  <span id="freeText7793835029700822524" style="display:none"><i>Sadie + Annabeth</i>, ultimate girl power!<br /><br />Wow, I'm literally hyperventilating right now because of how really great this book is. I mean, Rick Riordan writes so well. Simply the best. <br /><br />When I read the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17312201.The_Son_of_Sobek__Percy_Jackson___Kane_Chronicles_Crossover___1_" title="The Son of Sobek (Percy Jackson &amp; Kane Chronicles Crossover, #1) by Rick Riordan" rel="nofollow noopener">The Son of Sobek</a>, I was really amazed by the crossover. Two of my favorite fictional crushes combined? That is what you call fantastic.<br /><br />And then I read this book. Oh gods, I couldn't ask for more. It was really a great read, two different worlds are combined into a single story. Perfect.<br /><br />I really hope Rick is working on another crossover series which involves <b>all of the characters</b> from <i>Kane Chronicles</i>, <i>Percy Jackson and the Olympians</i>, and <i>The Heroes of Olympus</i>. I'm craving for more! <br /><br />All in all, this is really an amazing read.</span>

<div id="review_1077189497" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1077189497" />
    <a title="Karlé" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12198601-karl"><img alt="Karlé" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572287076p2/12198601.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1077189497?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karlé" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karlé" href="/user/show/12198601-karl">Karlé</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1077189497" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15492366428744860641">Thank all the gods for this crossover!! I really want to read <i>The Kane Chronicles</i> but I couldn't find any motivation. <i>The Son of Sobek</i> really impressed me, but this.. wow. This opened my heart, my body and my soul to a whole new world. Just like Annabeth, I'm in awe. Rick Riordan is truly the Myth Master!!<br/><br/><br/><b>100 POINTS FOR SADIEBETH!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412994411ra/11453859.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></span>
  <span id="freeText15492366428744860641" style="display:none">Thank all the gods for this crossover!! I really want to read <i>The Kane Chronicles</i> but I couldn't find any motivation. <i>The Son of Sobek</i> really impressed me, but this.. wow. This opened my heart, my body and my soul to a whole new world. Just like Annabeth, I'm in awe. Rick Riordan is truly the Myth Master!!<br><br><br><b>100 POINTS FOR SADIEBETH!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412994411ra/11453859.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="15492366428744860641" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b5wTEMMj1SI+4+k1o7b4ZgZS+w1uNLZwghyLuMU40Jt34LBIiRmR+4lWPgZxiGcNhNy1JGecJjJJJ7XpADCh2g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('me20p/3CP90PqP23mRFzCBs3tygUk5I7mvwB+S4AcJWBkRf/t/h7BLgdKoRLL+xjmbn5AR07AnlRxz+o6wgB1A==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/26641852-the-staff-of-serapis-percy-jackson-kane-chronicles-crossover-2">Quotes from The Staff of Serapis</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;This was a few weeks ago," Annabeth said. "Percy told me a crazy story about meeting a boy our near Moriches Bay. Apparently this kid used hieroglyphs to cast spells. He helped Percy battle a crocodile monsters."<br /><br />"The Sob of Sobek!" Sadie blurted. "But my <i>brother</i> battled that monster. He didn't say anything about-"<br /><br />"Is your brother's name Carter?" Annabeth asked.<br /><br />An angry golden aura flickered around Sadie's head-a halo of hieroglyphs that resembled frowns, fists, and dead stick men.<br /><br />"As of this moment," Sadie growled, "My brother's name is Punching Bag.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/1217541-this-was-a-few-weeks-ago-annabeth-said-percy-told">58 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Oh, I believe you. It’s too ridiculous not to be true. It’s just that each time my world gets stranger, I think: Right. We’re at maximum oddness now. At least I know the full extent of it. First, I find out my brother and I are descended from the pharaohs and have magic powers. All right. No problem. Then I find out my dead father has merged his soul with Osiris and Why not? Then my uncle takes over the House of Life and oversees hundreds of magicians around the world. Then my boyfriend turns out to be a hybrid magician boy/immortal god of funerals. And all the while I’m thinking, Of course! Keep calm and carry on! I’ve adjusted! And then you come along on a random Thursday, la-di-da, and say, Oh, by the way, Egyptian gods are just one small part of the cosmic absurdity. We’ve also got the Greeks to worry about! Hooray! &rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
